!= nil {\n639: \t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"verify JWT failed\", zap.Error(err))\n640: \t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n641: \t\t}\n642: \t\t\t// for example, someone may alter the auth plugin name but forgot to change the password...\n650: \t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Warn(\"verify through LDAP SASL failed\", zap.String(\"username\", user.Username), zap.Error(err))\n651: \t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n652: \t\t}\n653: \t} else if record.AuthPlugin == len(authentication) > 0 {\n670: \t\tswitch record.AuthPlugin {\n671: \t\t// NOTE: If the checking of the clear-text password fails, please set `info.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true`.\n672: \t\tcase \t\t\t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n677: \t\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n678: \t\t\t}\n679: \n680: \t\t\tif record.AuthPlugin)\n686: \t\t\tif err != nil {\n687: \t\t\t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(\"Failed to check caching_sha2_password\", zap.Error(err))\n688: \t\t\t}\n689: \n690: \t\t\tif !authok {\n691: \t\t\t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n692: \t\t\t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n693: \t\t\t}\n694: \t\tdefault:\n695: ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n697: \t\t}\n698: \t} else if len(pwd) > 0 || len(authentication) > 0 {\n699: \t\tinfo.FailedDueToWrongPassword = true\n700: \t\treturn info, ErrAccessDenied.FastGenByArgs(user.Username, user.Hostname, hasPassword)\n701: \t}\n702: \n703: \t// Login a locked account is not allowed.\n704: \tlocked := record.AccountLocked\n705: \tif locked {\n706: \t\tlogutil.BgLogger().Error(fmt.Sprintf(\"Access denied for authUser '%s'@'%s'.
